FROM project AS p

LEFT JOIN customer AS c ON p.customerid = c.customerid
LEFT JOIN projecttype AS p0 ON p.projecttypeid = p0.projecttypeid
LEFT JOIN subpractice AS s0 ON p.subpracticeid = s0.subpracticeid
LEFT JOIN practice AS p1 ON s0.practiceid = p1.practiceid

SELECT c.customerid, c.firstname, c.lastname, CASE
    WHEN c.companyname = '' THEN (COALESCE(c.firstname, '') || ' ') || COALESCE(c.lastname, '')
    ELSE c.companyname
END, (c.companylogourl IS NULL) OR c.companylogourl = '', c.companylogourl, c.pannumber, c.gstnumber, c.companyemail, COALESCE(c.phone1, ''), COALESCE(c.address1, ''), COALESCE(c.zipcode, ''), p.paymenttermid IS NULL, p.paymenttermid, p.paymenttermname, c0.currencyid IS NULL, c0.currencyid, c0.currencyname, c1.cityid IS NULL, c1.cityid, c1.cityname, (
    SELECT count(*)::int
    FROM project AS p0
    WHERE c.customerid = p0.customerid), t."ProjectId", t."ProjectName", t."TotalEmployees", t."TotalAmount", t."ProjectStatus", t.statusid
FROM customer AS c
LEFT JOIN paymentterm AS p ON c.paymenttermid = p.paymenttermid
LEFT JOIN currency AS c0 ON c.currencyid = c0.currencyid
LEFT JOIN city AS c1 ON c.cityid = c1.cityid
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT p1.projectid AS "ProjectId", COALESCE(p1.projectname, '') AS "ProjectName", (
        SELECT count(*)::int
        FROM projectcontract AS p2
        INNER JOIN contractemployee AS c2 ON p2.contractid = c2.contractid
        WHERE p1.projectid = p2.projectid AND c2.categorysubstatusid IN (5, 6, 4, 3, 2) AND c2.contractid = COALESCE((
            SELECT p3.contractid
            FROM projectcontract AS p3
            WHERE p1.projectid = p3.projectid
            LIMIT 1), 0)) AS "TotalEmployees", (
        SELECT COALESCE(sum(p4.amount), 0.0)
        FROM projectcontract AS p4
        WHERE p1.projectid = p4.projectid) AS "TotalAmount", s.statusname AS "ProjectStatus", s.statusid, p1.customerid
    FROM project AS p1
    LEFT JOIN status AS s ON p1.statusid = s.statusid
) AS t ON c.customerid = t.customerid
WHERE (c.isdeleted <> TRUE OR (c.isdeleted IS NULL)) AND (c.isactive <> FALSE OR (c.isactive IS NULL))
ORDER BY c.customerid, p.paymenttermid, c0.currencyid, c1.cityid, t."ProjectId"

END, (

    FROM costsheetdetail AS c2

SELECT t.costsheetid, t.costsheetname, t0."Costsheetdetailid", t0."Costsheetid", t0."Skillid", t0.skillexperience, t0."Requiredresource", t0."Skillcost", t0."Skillname", t0."Xvalue", t0."Perioddays", t0."Customerprice", t0."Totalcost", t0."Totalprice", t0.skillid0, t.c, t.c0, t.c1, t1.costsheetid, t1.version, t1."Costsheetdetailid", t1."Costsheetid0", t1."Skillid", t1.skillexperience, t1."Requiredresource", t1."Skillcost", t1."Skillname", t1."Xvalue", t1."Perioddays", t1."Customerprice", t1."Totalcost", t1."Totalprice", t1.skillid0
FROM (
    SELECT c.costsheetid, c.costsheetname, (
        SELECT avg(COALESCE(c0.xvalue, 0.0))
        FROM costsheetdetail AS c0
        WHERE c.costsheetid = c0.costsheetid) AS c, CASE
        WHEN EXISTS (
            SELECT 1
            FROM oaf AS o
            WHERE c.costsheetid = o.costsheetid) THEN (
            SELECT o0.oafid
            FROM oaf AS o0
            WHERE c.costsheetid = o0.costsheetid
            LIMIT 1)
        ELSE NULL
    END AS c0, CASE
        WHEN EXISTS (
            SELECT 1
            FROM oaf AS o1
            WHERE c.costsheetid = o1.costsheetid) THEN (
            SELECT o2.orderdescription
            FROM oaf AS o2
            WHERE c.costsheetid = o2.costsheetid
            LIMIT 1)
        ELSE NULL
    END AS c1
    FROM costsheet AS c
    WHERE c.costsheetid = @__id_0
    LIMIT 1
) AS t
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT c1.costsheetdetailid AS "Costsheetdetailid", c1.costsheetid AS "Costsheetid", c1.skillid AS "Skillid", c1.skillexperince AS skillexperience, c1.requiredresource AS "Requiredresource", c1.skillcost AS "Skillcost", s.skillname AS "Skillname", c1.xvalue AS "Xvalue", c1.perioddays AS "Perioddays", c1.customerprice AS "Customerprice", c1.totalcost AS "Totalcost", c1.totalprice AS "Totalprice", s.skillid AS skillid0
    FROM costsheetdetail AS c1
    INNER JOIN skill AS s ON c1.skillid = s.skillid
) AS t0 ON t.costsheetid = t0."Costsheetid"
LEFT JOIN LATERAL (
    SELECT t2.costsheetid, t2.version, t3."Costsheetdetailid", t3."Costsheetid" AS "Costsheetid0", t3."Skillid", t3.skillexperience, t3."Requiredresource", t3."Skillcost", t3."Skillname", t3."Xvalue", t3."Perioddays", t3."Customerprice", t3."Totalcost", t3."Totalprice", t3.skillid0
    FROM (
        SELECT c2.costsheetid, c2.version
        FROM costsheetdetail_history AS c2
        WHERE t.costsheetid = c2.costsheetid
        GROUP BY c2.costsheetid, c2.version
    ) AS t2
    LEFT JOIN (
        SELECT c3.costsheetdetailid AS "Costsheetdetailid", c3.costsheetid AS "Costsheetid", c3.skillid AS "Skillid", c3.skillexperince AS skillexperience, c3.requiredresource AS "Requiredresource", c3.skillcost AS "Skillcost", s0.skillname AS "Skillname", c3.xvalue AS "Xvalue", c3.perioddays AS "Perioddays", c3.customerprice AS "Customerprice", c3.totalcost AS "Totalcost", c3.totalprice AS "Totalprice", s0.skillid AS skillid0, c3.version
        FROM costsheetdetail_history AS c3
        INNER JOIN skill AS s0 ON c3.skillid = s0.skillid
        WHERE t.costsheetid = c3.costsheetid
    ) AS t3 ON t2.costsheetid = t3."Costsheetid" AND (t2.version = t3.version OR ((t2.version IS NULL) AND (t3.version IS NULL)))
) AS t1 ON TRUE
ORDER BY t.costsheetid, t0."Costsheetdetailid", t0.skillid0, t1.costsheetid, t1.version, t1."Costsheetdetailid"

SELECT c.customerid, c.firstname, c.lastname, CASE
    WHEN c.companyname = '' THEN (COALESCE(c.firstname, '') || ' ') || COALESCE(c.lastname, '')
    ELSE c.companyname
END, (c.companylogourl IS NULL) OR c.companylogourl = '', c.companylogourl, c.pannumber, c.gstnumber, c.companyemail, COALESCE(c.phone1, ''), COALESCE(c.address1, ''), COALESCE(c.zipcode, ''), p.paymenttermid IS NULL, p.paymenttermid, p.paymenttermname, c0.currencyid IS NULL, c0.currencyid, c0.currencyname, c1.cityid IS NULL, c1.cityid, c1.cityname, (
    SELECT count(*)::int
    FROM project AS p0
    WHERE c.customerid = p0.customerid), t."ProjectId", t."ProjectName", t."TotalEmployees", t."TotalAmount", t."ProjectStatus", t.statusid
FROM customer AS c
LEFT JOIN paymentterm AS p ON c.paymenttermid = p.paymenttermid
LEFT JOIN currency AS c0 ON c.currencyid = c0.currencyid
LEFT JOIN city AS c1 ON c.cityid = c1.cityid
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT p1.projectid AS "ProjectId", COALESCE(p1.projectname, '') AS "ProjectName", (
        SELECT count(*)::int
        FROM projectcontract AS p2
        INNER JOIN contractemployee AS c2 ON p2.contractid = c2.contractid
        WHERE p1.projectid = p2.projectid AND c2.categorysubstatusid IN (5, 6, 4, 3, 2) AND c2.contractid = COALESCE((
            SELECT p3.contractid
            FROM projectcontract AS p3
            WHERE p1.projectid = p3.projectid
            LIMIT 1), 0)) AS "TotalEmployees", (
        SELECT COALESCE(sum(p4.amount), 0.0)
        FROM projectcontract AS p4
        WHERE p1.projectid = p4.projectid) AS "TotalAmount", s.statusname AS "ProjectStatus", s.statusid, p1.customerid
    FROM project AS p1
    LEFT JOIN status AS s ON p1.statusid = s.statusid
) AS t ON c.customerid = t.customerid
WHERE (c.isdeleted <> TRUE OR (c.isdeleted IS NULL)) AND (c.isactive <> FALSE OR (c.isactive IS NULL))
ORDER BY c.customerid, p.paymenttermid, c0.currencyid, c1.cityid, t."ProjectId"

SELECT c.customerid, c.firstname, c.lastname, CASE
    WHEN c.companyname = '' THEN (COALESCE(c.firstname, '') || ' ') || COALESCE(c.lastname, '')
    ELSE c.companyname
END, (c.companylogourl IS NULL) OR c.companylogourl = '', c.companylogourl, c.pannumber, c.gstnumber, c.companyemail, COALESCE(c.phone1, ''), COALESCE(c.address1, ''), COALESCE(c.zipcode, ''), p.paymenttermid IS NULL, p.paymenttermid, p.paymenttermname, c0.currencyid IS NULL, c0.currencyid, c0.currencyname, c1.cityid IS NULL, c1.cityid, c1.cityname, (
    SELECT count(*)::int
    FROM project AS p0
    WHERE c.customerid = p0.customerid), t."ProjectId", t."ProjectName", t."TotalEmployees", t."TotalAmount", t."ProjectStatus", t.statusid
FROM customer AS c
LEFT JOIN paymentterm AS p ON c.paymenttermid = p.paymenttermid
LEFT JOIN currency AS c0 ON c.currencyid = c0.currencyid
LEFT JOIN city AS c1 ON c.cityid = c1.cityid
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT p1.projectid AS "ProjectId", COALESCE(p1.projectname, '') AS "ProjectName", (
        SELECT count(*)::int
        FROM projectcontract AS p2
        INNER JOIN contractemployee AS c2 ON p2.contractid = c2.contractid
        WHERE p1.projectid = p2.projectid AND c2.categorysubstatusid IN (5, 6, 4, 3, 2) AND c2.contractid = COALESCE((
            SELECT p3.contractid
            FROM projectcontract AS p3
            WHERE p1.projectid = p3.projectid
            LIMIT 1), 0)) AS "TotalEmployees", (
        SELECT COALESCE(sum(p4.amount), 0.0)
        FROM projectcontract AS p4
        WHERE p1.projectid = p4.projectid) AS "TotalAmount", s.statusname AS "ProjectStatus", s.statusid, p1.customerid
    FROM project AS p1
    LEFT JOIN status AS s ON p1.statusid = s.statusid
) AS t ON c.customerid = t.customerid
WHERE (c.isdeleted <> TRUE OR (c.isdeleted IS NULL)) AND (c.isactive <> FALSE OR (c.isactive IS NULL))

SELECT c.customerid, c.firstname, c.lastname, CASE
    WHEN c.companyname = '' THEN (COALESCE(c.firstname, '') || ' ') || COALESCE(c.lastname, '')
    ELSE c.companyname
END, (c.companylogourl IS NULL) OR c.companylogourl = '', c.companylogourl, c.pannumber, c.gstnumber, c.companyemail, COALESCE(c.phone1, ''), COALESCE(c.address1, ''), COALESCE(c.zipcode, ''), p.paymenttermid IS NULL, p.paymenttermid, p.paymenttermname, c0.currencyid IS NULL, c0.currencyid, c0.currencyname, c1.cityid IS NULL, c1.cityid, c1.cityname, (
    SELECT count(*)::int
    FROM project AS p0
    WHERE c.customerid = p0.customerid), t."ProjectId", t."ProjectName", t."TotalEmployees", t."TotalAmount", t."ProjectStatus", t.statusid
FROM customer AS c
LEFT JOIN paymentterm AS p ON c.paymenttermid = p.paymenttermid
LEFT JOIN currency AS c0 ON c.currencyid = c0.currencyid
LEFT JOIN city AS c1 ON c.cityid = c1.cityid
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT p1.projectid AS "ProjectId", COALESCE(p1.projectname, '') AS "ProjectName", (
        SELECT count(*)::int
        FROM projectcontract AS p2
        INNER JOIN contractemployee AS c2 ON p2.contractid = c2.contractid
        WHERE p1.projectid = p2.projectid AND c2.categorysubstatusid IN (5, 6, 4, 3, 2) AND c2.contractid = COALESCE((
            SELECT p3.contractid
            FROM projectcontract AS p3
            WHERE p1.projectid = p3.projectid
            LIMIT 1), 0)) AS "TotalEmployees", (
        SELECT COALESCE(sum(p4.amount), 0.0)
        FROM projectcontract AS p4
        WHERE p1.projectid = p4.projectid) AS "TotalAmount", s.statusname AS "ProjectStatus", s.statusid, p1.customerid
    FROM project AS p1
    LEFT JOIN status AS s ON p1.statusid = s.statusid
) AS t ON c.customerid = t.customerid
WHERE (c.isdeleted <> TRUE OR (c.isdeleted IS NULL)) AND (c.isactive <> FALSE OR (c.isactive IS NULL))
ORDER BY c.customerid, p.paymenttermid, c0.currencyid, c1.cityid, t."ProjectId"

SELECT c.customerid, c.firstname, c.lastname, CASE
    WHEN c.companyname = '' THEN (COALESCE(c.firstname, '') || ' ') || COALESCE(c.lastname, '')
    ELSE c.companyname
END, (c.companylogourl IS NULL) OR c.companylogourl = '', c.companylogourl, c.pannumber, c.gstnumber, c.companyemail, COALESCE(c.phone1, ''), COALESCE(c.address1, ''), COALESCE(c.zipcode, ''), p.paymenttermid IS NULL, p.paymenttermid, p.paymenttermname, c0.currencyid IS NULL, c0.currencyid, c0.currencyname, c1.cityid IS NULL, c1.cityid, c1.cityname, (
    SELECT count(*)::int
    FROM project AS p0
    WHERE c.customerid = p0.customerid), t."ProjectId", t."ProjectName", t."TotalEmployees", t."TotalAmount", t."ProjectStatus", t.statusid
FROM customer AS c
LEFT JOIN paymentterm AS p ON c.paymenttermid = p.paymenttermid
LEFT JOIN currency AS c0 ON c.currencyid = c0.currencyid
LEFT JOIN city AS c1 ON c.cityid = c1.cityid
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT p1.projectid AS "ProjectId", COALESCE(p1.projectname, '') AS "ProjectName", (
        SELECT count(*)::int
        FROM projectcontract AS p2
        INNER JOIN contractemployee AS c2 ON p2.contractid = c2.contractid
        WHERE p1.projectid = p2.projectid AND c2.categorysubstatusid IN (5, 6, 4, 3, 2) AND c2.contractid = COALESCE((
            SELECT p3.contractid
            FROM projectcontract AS p3
            WHERE p1.projectid = p3.projectid
            LIMIT 1), 0)) AS "TotalEmployees", (
        SELECT COALESCE(sum(p4.amount), 0.0)
        FROM projectcontract AS p4
        WHERE p1.projectid = p4.projectid) AS "TotalAmount", s.statusname AS "ProjectStatus", s.statusid, p1.customerid
    FROM project AS p1
    LEFT JOIN status AS s ON p1.statusid = s.statusid
) AS t ON c.customerid = t.customerid
WHERE (c.isdeleted <> TRUE OR (c.isdeleted IS NULL)) AND (c.isactive <> FALSE OR (c.isactive IS NULL))
ORDER BY c.customerid, p.paymenttermid, c0.currencyid, c1.cityid, t."ProjectId"

SELECT c.customerid, c.firstname, c.lastname, CASE
    WHEN c.companyname = '' THEN (COALESCE(c.firstname, '') || ' ') || COALESCE(c.lastname, '')
    ELSE c.companyname
END, (c.companylogourl IS NULL) OR c.companylogourl = '', c.companylogourl, c.pannumber, c.gstnumber, c.companyemail, COALESCE(c.phone1, ''), COALESCE(c.address1, ''), COALESCE(c.zipcode, ''), p.paymenttermid IS NULL, p.paymenttermid, p.paymenttermname, c0.currencyid IS NULL, c0.currencyid, c0.currencyname, c1.cityid IS NULL, c1.cityid, c1.cityname, (
    SELECT count(*)::int
    FROM project AS p0
    WHERE c.customerid = p0.customerid), t."ProjectId", t."ProjectName", t."TotalEmployees", t."TotalAmount", t."ProjectStatus", t.statusid
FROM customer AS c
LEFT JOIN paymentterm AS p ON c.paymenttermid = p.paymenttermid
LEFT JOIN currency AS c0 ON c.currencyid = c0.currencyid
LEFT JOIN city AS c1 ON c.cityid = c1.cityid
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT p1.projectid AS "ProjectId", COALESCE(p1.projectname, '') AS "ProjectName", (
        SELECT count(*)::int
        FROM projectcontract AS p2
        INNER JOIN contractemployee AS c2 ON p2.contractid = c2.contractid
        WHERE p1.projectid = p2.projectid AND c2.categorysubstatusid IN (5, 6, 4, 3, 2) AND c2.contractid = COALESCE((
            SELECT p3.contractid
            FROM projectcontract AS p3
            WHERE p1.projectid = p3.projectid
            LIMIT 1), 0)) AS "TotalEmployees", (
        SELECT COALESCE(sum(p4.amount), 0.0)
        FROM projectcontract AS p4
        WHERE p1.projectid = p4.projectid) AS "TotalAmount", s.statusname AS "ProjectStatus", s.statusid, p1.customerid
    FROM project AS p1
    LEFT JOIN status AS s ON p1.statusid = s.statusid
) AS t ON c.customerid = t.customerid
WHERE (c.isdeleted <> TRUE OR (c.isdeleted IS NULL)) AND (c.isactive <> FALSE OR (c.isactive IS NULL))
ORDER BY c.customerid, p.paymenttermid, c0.currencyid, c1.cityid, t."ProjectId"

SELECT c.customerid AS "CustomerId", CASE
    WHEN c.companyname = '' THEN (COALESCE(c.firstname, '') || ' ') || COALESCE(c.lastname, '')
    ELSE c.companyname
END AS "CustomerCompanyName"
FROM customer AS c
WHERE EXISTS (
    SELECT 1
    FROM project AS p
    WHERE c.customerid = p.customerid AND EXISTS (
        SELECT 1
        FROM projectcontract AS p0
        WHERE p.projectid = p0.projectid AND EXISTS (
            SELECT 1
            FROM contractemployee AS c0
            WHERE p0.contractid = c0.contractid AND c0.employeeid = @__employeeId_0) AND (p0.statusid <> 6 OR (p0.statusid IS NULL))))

SELECT c.customerid, c.firstname, c.lastname, CASE
    WHEN c.companyname = '' THEN (COALESCE(c.firstname, '') || ' ') || COALESCE(c.lastname, '')
    ELSE c.companyname
END, (c.companylogourl IS NULL) OR c.companylogourl = '', c.companylogourl, c.pannumber, c.gstnumber, c.companyemail, COALESCE(c.phone1, ''), COALESCE(c.address1, ''), COALESCE(c.zipcode, ''), p.paymenttermid IS NULL, p.paymenttermid, p.paymenttermname, c0.currencyid IS NULL, c0.currencyid, c0.currencyname, c1.cityid IS NULL, c1.cityid, c1.cityname, (
    SELECT count(*)::int
    FROM project AS p0
    WHERE c.customerid = p0.customerid), t."ProjectId", t."ProjectName", t."TotalEmployees", t."TotalAmount", t."ProjectStatus", t.statusid
FROM customer AS c
LEFT JOIN paymentterm AS p ON c.paymenttermid = p.paymenttermid
LEFT JOIN currency AS c0 ON c.currencyid = c0.currencyid
LEFT JOIN city AS c1 ON c.cityid = c1.cityid
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT p1.projectid AS "ProjectId", COALESCE(p1.projectname, '') AS "ProjectName", (
        SELECT count(*)::int
        FROM projectcontract AS p2
        INNER JOIN contractemployee AS c2 ON p2.contractid = c2.contractid
        WHERE p1.projectid = p2.projectid AND c2.categorysubstatusid IN (5, 6, 4, 3, 2) AND c2.contractid = COALESCE((
            SELECT p3.contractid
            FROM projectcontract AS p3
            WHERE p1.projectid = p3.projectid
            LIMIT 1), 0)) AS "TotalEmployees", (
        SELECT COALESCE(sum(p4.amount), 0.0)
        FROM projectcontract AS p4
        WHERE p1.projectid = p4.projectid) AS "TotalAmount", s.statusname AS "ProjectStatus", s.statusid, p1.customerid
    FROM project AS p1
    LEFT JOIN status AS s ON p1.statusid = s.statusid
) AS t ON c.customerid = t.customerid
WHERE (c.isdeleted <> TRUE OR (c.isdeleted IS NULL)) AND (c.isactive <> FALSE OR (c.isactive IS NULL))
ORDER BY c.customerid, p.paymenttermid, c0.currencyid, c1.cityid, t."ProjectId"

SELECT c.customerid, c.firstname, c.lastname, CASE
    WHEN c.companyname = '' THEN (COALESCE(c.firstname, '') || ' ') || COALESCE(c.lastname, '')
    ELSE c.companyname
END, (c.companylogourl IS NULL) OR c.companylogourl = '', c.companylogourl, c.pannumber, c.gstnumber, c.companyemail, COALESCE(c.phone1, ''), COALESCE(c.address1, ''), COALESCE(c.zipcode, ''), p.paymenttermid IS NULL, p.paymenttermid, p.paymenttermname, c0.currencyid IS NULL, c0.currencyid, c0.currencyname, c1.cityid IS NULL, c1.cityid, c1.cityname, (
    SELECT count(*)::int
    FROM project AS p0
    WHERE c.customerid = p0.customerid), t."ProjectId", t."ProjectName", t."TotalEmployees", t."TotalAmount", t."ProjectStatus", t.statusid
FROM customer AS c
LEFT JOIN paymentterm AS p ON c.paymenttermid = p.paymenttermid
LEFT JOIN currency AS c0 ON c.currencyid = c0.currencyid
LEFT JOIN city AS c1 ON c.cityid = c1.cityid
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT p1.projectid AS "ProjectId", COALESCE(p1.projectname, '') AS "ProjectName", (
        SELECT count(*)::int
        FROM projectcontract AS p2
        INNER JOIN contractemployee AS c2 ON p2.contractid = c2.contractid
        WHERE p1.projectid = p2.projectid AND c2.categorysubstatusid IN (5, 6, 4, 3, 2) AND c2.contractid = COALESCE((
            SELECT p3.contractid
            FROM projectcontract AS p3
            WHERE p1.projectid = p3.projectid
            LIMIT 1), 0)) AS "TotalEmployees", (
        SELECT COALESCE(sum(p4.amount), 0.0)
        FROM projectcontract AS p4
        WHERE p1.projectid = p4.projectid) AS "TotalAmount", s.statusname AS "ProjectStatus", s.statusid, p1.customerid
    FROM project AS p1
    LEFT JOIN status AS s ON p1.statusid = s.statusid
) AS t ON c.customerid = t.customerid
WHERE (c.isdeleted <> TRUE OR (c.isdeleted IS NULL)) AND (c.isactive <> FALSE OR (c.isactive IS NULL))
ORDER BY c.customerid, p.paymenttermid, c0.currencyid, c1.cityid, t."ProjectId"
